15/02/22, 11:43 pm - Sujit Khade (KJ Clg): Hello there,

We are team hell god. Our topic is No poverty

Our team members are Chaitanya Kumbhar who's our team lead,Shivraj Yewale,Prathamesh Adsul And lastly me Sujit Khaade dont ask why i used an AI's Voice. we all are first year students of KJ's Trinity college and institutes.

so you all must be wondering why we chose this topic the world population, lived in extreme poverty, struggling to fulfil the most basic needs like health, education and access to water and sanitation, to name a few. However, the COVID-19 pandemic is reversing the trend of poverty reduction with tens of millions of people in risk of being pushed back into extreme poverty people living on less than $1.90/day. causing the first increase in global poverty in more than 20 years. Our main goal is to end poverty in all its forms everywhere by 2030.Over 830 million people live below the International Extreme Poverty line of $1.90 a day. Our Idea is to build a website and application that is ‘You Are Hired’ a platform where those people want's job & those who want's employees in less salary both can apply & communicate with each other directly. Both can create profile and explain about their job description. It will be great platform for unemployed one and also for the recruiters to exchanging remuneration. On our website or app employee & companies both can make profile. Talented unemployed who mastered their skill but don’t have certificate can find suitable work for their skills by qualifying test provided by us. Companies will mention all details about their work & those who have suitable profile they can get hired. An applicant can work on a variety of projects at the same time but for different clients. A candidate can work from anywhere globally, and in given times, it mainly involves work from home. It’s really one of the simplest and most pure forms of entrepreneurship: the applicant provides a specific service or outcome, and the buyer pays them a fee directly. There are lots of Google software's out there that can improve and modify your skills. Such as Google cloud, In Google cloud you can apply for any courses for free of cost After completing a course and exam you will get a badge and you can mention that badge in your resume so that will make your resume even more strong. And there are also other software's like Firebase,Flutter,Tensor Flow. So i hope you all will understand what's the main reason for poverty and how we can solve that that's all from the team Hell god. I hope you guys like it. Thank you.

अंतर्गत पंतप्रधान मा. श्री. नरेंद्र मोदी यांच्या आवाहनानुसार रामलल्ला मूर्ती प्रतिष्ठापणे निमित्त गावातील सर्व मंदिराच्या आजूबाजूचा परिसर स्वच्छ करण्यात आला. तसेच प्रतिष्ठापणे दिवशी मंदिरात दिव्यांची 01/02/24, 1:10 pm - CK: The special labor awareness camp of the National Service Scheme at the Trinity College of Engineering and Research, Bopdev Ghat, Pune, took place from January 20 to 26, 2024. Various activities such as population control, awareness on mobile usage, lectures on Shivaji Maharaj's administration, and talks on historical figures like Shambhu Charitra and Swatantryaveer Savarkar were organized during the camp. Additionally, voluntary work such as cleanliness campaigns, guidance for school students, population control, temple cleaning, and cultural programs were carried out. The program also included the cleanliness of the surroundings of all temples in the village as part of the invitation from Prime Minister Narendra Modi for the installation of the Ram Lalla idol. The inauguration was attended by the college principal, village head, and other local dignitaries. The camp's closing ceremony involved the participation of various community members and former students who contributed to its success. Around 50 boys and girls actively participated in the program, making it a successful endeavor.
